Amazing breakfast spot!
Ordered the Java combo with Waffle. Everything tasted great, their house potatoes are quite good, the atmosphere is cozy yet refreshing all with a small cafe vibe. Really enjoyed eating here and the prices are on par with other dinner chains. Why not rather support a family owned business where the owner takes pride in his food and restaurant.< /text>

Phillip Butler< /username>
<time>1568721010808< /time>< rating>
4<//rating>
< text>
I was complaining a bit at the price which was 38 for two cheeseburgers and fries but oh my... this is honestly the best burger I have had ever!!!!  Or a close equal to True Burger in Sherman Oaks, CA . I do not like fancy burgers and even though they have fancy burgers and an appearance of a tall height burger.. the taste is perfect! The meat was cooked to perfection, slightly pink inside and not dried out. The scampi fries smelled and tasted amazing although I probably didn't smell so good after eating some as they are loaded full of garlic, chili flakes and lemon. This place is very small, no seats inside and it appears people order burgers and eat at the bar next door. They have a couple small tables outside which I sat at. Great place if you are craving a really good burger!

Jumpin Java</text>

I‚Äôve been there a lot in the last 20 years living in my Studio City neighborhood.

I hadn‚Äôt tried the pancakes until this banner day.!
They are huge; I couldn‚Äôt finish the half order of 2. Real butter & maple syrup.

They have daily specials . Best BLT
Around with sides of fresh fruit or these special spiced potatoes!
And the sausage side is so good whether pork or turkey.

I‚Äôve tried pasta specials for lunch with a very veggie green salad.

I made this account specifically to write this review and maybe more down the line. The Manager here should be fired! Food is great. But please, whoever owns this joint needs to find a new Manager. I have never been treated so rudely and with such disrespect by a fellow human being in my life. I explained to the guy that the potatoes can not go on top of a waffle. The sauce and spice they cook the potatoes in soak into waffle. Rendering the my Belgium Waffle experience less than satisfying. I asked the Manager if he would make a new waffle or compensate me in some way...After all I have ordered here numerous time. He told me he would give me $2 then lectured me how I need to tell them not to put potatoes on the my Belgium Waffle. I explained kindly how down the line other customers should not have to go through the same thing as I did. That an easy fix would be to put them in a separate containers. He argued with me for no reason, and said to me, "Do you want the $2 or not". I wanted to tell him he can take his $2 and shove it where the sun don't shine, but instead I said "If this was my restaurant I would just comp the whole thing" in which he replied "I'll give you 50% off" and then immediately hung up on me. I did not want to write this review, but I feel as if there are far too many people looking for good work like a Manger position. This guy certainly does not deserve it. Maybe he was having a bad day, and I'll see a response here, but I doubt it. Good food though :)< /text>

< review>
95% of the time . . . . I often eat out, no restaurant is perfect! . . . . I eat breakfast/brunch at Jumpin Java most weekends, the wait is usually no more than 10-15min, the owner/s and  staff, most have worked there for years, are quite friendly-not solicitous, when I remember I call ahead and ask to be put on the waiting list, then when I arrived there's hardly a wait. The menu has a nice variety of choices, the food is fresh and served hot. And their prices are quite reasonable. If they do make a mistake, they rectify it with no attitude. FIVE STARS!!!!< /review>

of what I find interesting. In the past twenty-five years I must have visited over 150 Jewelry, Loan and Pawn shops in various states around the US and vintage boutiques in Europe.
From my first experience with the owner Yev Goldman and his entire staff, I have never been treated with a level of service which one would expect buying a 18k Gold Minute Repeater at the Vacheron Constantin Boutique on Rodeo or a 18K White Gold Paul Newman Daytona.
To call Yev's Jewelry & Loan a pawn shop, would belittle the boutique and the dedicated hard working staff. I have done both, purchased watches at a very fair price and loaned watches or other pieces in order to have immediate access to cash, if  exceptionally good deal on a watch or  collectors item was needed within hours. They have given me the opportunity to expand my collection at the best interest rates I have ever experienced. Most important is their integrity, they have educated me on pieces I overpaid and gave me advice not to purchase pieces that wouldn't hold value. I have never had a Jewelry or Watch store tell me that if I am buying a certain piece to re-sell at later time for a profit, not to do so, unless I truly liked the piece for myself and would keep it in my collection. <Rating>5<//Rating><Review>Update only to say we keep coming back here and are always happy that we did  this place is outstanding!

I just love this place! From the high quality of the seafood and the size of the portions to the staff who work there.

Not so easy to see from the street to keep aware but it does have a parking lot shared with a couple of other stores in the strip, I've seen it quite full but haven't had a problem finding a spot to park.

< time>

<rating>3</rating><Review>This playground is great for kids 3 and under. It's okay for kids older than that. The main equipment is basically one long, elevated platform with little "towers" every 30 ft or so that get progressively higher off the ground with a covered slide at the end. Each tower has different ways to climb up/down it like rope ladders, poles, etc. There is a semi-circle device that is basically a modern version of a teeter totter and probably was once pretty great, but it's so weathered and worn that there is too much friction for it to be much fun for any kid under about 10 (and how many kids that age come here?!). There is a zip line, though it's the sanitized version where it's on a metal track and very short with hardly any elevation change so pretty lackluster. There are toddler/baby swings as well as 2 regular swings and a merry-go-round with rope tower; all pretty standard playground stiff. There is a little climbing wall that uses actual faux rock instead of holds, but I have no idea who the target audience is because it's way too hard for any kid who would be of the age that they would be coming to this program.

Finally, this playground has an interesting vibe because it's buried behind houses and hence removed from a road which makes it somewhat peaceful. It's also basically built into the side of a steep hill, so one side effectively has a wall of earth (with lots of plants and stairs up to the Rec Center).

Overall, this is a pretty average park in a neighborhood, St. Mary's Park, that not many people visit or know about, so worth  checking out if you're not from the immediate area as a way to try a new playground with the kids.<//Review><pics>None</pics>< Resp>
None</Resp>

< text>
Good playground with a huge structure and lots of activities covering a good age range.  Bathrooms available most of the time at the rec center just up the hill.  Occasional drainage problems from problematic landscaping design choices, but nothing serious.  Supports a good age range.

Fenced all around, but there are a lot of easily-opened gates at different elevation levels and some vision blockers, so maintaining a perimeter around a group of kids requires several adults -- don't expect to be able to supervise from a single fixed location.< /text>

< review>
Nice clean location. Staff is quick and efficient. Jennifer was our waitress and she was awesome. Jennifer had a positive attitude and cracked jokes all the way. Her personality made our experience that much better. We have been to this location on multiple locations since their grand opening and the service has been outstanding. The food is awesome. Yes, there are some dishes that can improve such as; the spaghetti which is a bit or miss item (sometimes the sauce is watery and the noodles are over cooked), they don't have much of a salad bar, and their dessert bar is small and always out of chocolate covered items. Other than that their steak and roast beef is awesome, their grilled shrimp is tatesty, and their rotisserie  chicken is golden. Also, would be awesome, if they offered military discounts for active, veterans. and retired personnel.<//review>

Well, my son wanted to eat there for his B-day dinner. So after paying $60 for 4 of us we hoped it would be a great experience.
The good points: Staff were courteous, attentive, and full of welcoming smiles.üëç
Grilled sirloin steak quality was pretty good and grilled to ordered, the smoked hickory chicken & ribs were flavorful.
The Bad "Salty" points: Its a total shame that all the food mentioned above were all salty. All the starches like rice, potatoes were all salty. The only things not salty was the salad bar and dessert. I tried giving the benefit of the doubt so I tried the fried fish. And again, fish batter was salty and fish was salty. My wife and son all said the same thing. I decided to look up reviews during this Birthday meal and found out that NATIONWIDE(CA, AZ, SC) , all the reviews say the same SALTY theme. I should have looked at it prior to paying $60.
I've worked in the restaurant industry for 10 years and know that this is a tactic so that customers get fuller quicker once their body's salt level rises. If you have health conditions with blood pressure risks, please do not eat here. I urge the company to cut 40% of the salt on all the dishes. If they do, I'd gladly write a new review with 4's and 5 stars. I give a star for the great staff, and a star for fresh quality, but ‚Äîstars for making people pay there $15 and not only make them full quicker, but put in health risks. Please read other reviews before going here.

< username>
Donna Jones</username>
<Text>I can't understand the negative reviews I've read. Maybe customers who dined at GC when they first opened had a less than desirable experience.
Now for my experience.  My friend and I went to Murrieta GC for lunch on a Friday at around 11am, not too many people, but more came in closer to noon. It was our first time eating at a Golden Corral so it took a couple of minutes to get our bearings. After paying and getting our beverages we found a table and put utensils and napkins and drinks down.Before
choosing our food we scanned each section so we could see everything .We were so surprised at the variety of food offered!
Despite other reviews, there were at least 6 vegetables, all were piping hot and  cooked just right, not overcooked or undercooked.The baked potato were a nice touch, also nice and hot with sour cream and butter right there.
Numerous entrees were offered that should satisfy any taste. Even a taco bar and Chinese
food. I tried the pulled pork, it was tender, juicy,slightly smokey delicious! I also tried
the spaghetti. The sauce was tasty enough but the pasta had become very soft. My friend had tacos and pot roast which she liked very much.  So many more choices but you can't try everthing! Allthough the salad area was well stocked we decided not to fill up on salad but to save room for dessert. After reading previous reviews I didn't expect much from the dessert station but wow, what a surprise to see pecan pie,carrot cake, lemon meringue pie, red velvet
cake and too many others to mention. Between the two of us we tried the pecan pie, soft serve ice cream and turtle cheesecake. They were all great! To also refute prior reviews the restaurant was immaculate, food stations were frequently being wiped down as soon as necessary, our server was sweet and helpful and came by at least 3 times to see if we needed refills.As a couple of people have mentioned, it is a little pricy for lunch but considering the quality and variety well worth it! Anxious to bring my husband for dinner!
Puts Hometown Buffet to shame.</Text><Pictures>None</Pictures></record></dataset><record>
